[\[31b.6\]]gsung rab yan lag bcu gnyis kyi dbang gis kyang /_theg chen gyi sde snod gang du sdud pa der 'dus so/_/gnyis pa la gnyis las/_dang po gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa phar phyin theg pa las khyad par 'phags tshul ni/_khyad par bzhis

[\[32a.1\]]de bas na mdo sngags gnyis kyi khyad par dngos ni thabs dang spyod pa dag la yod pa yin gyi lta ba ni mtshungs so/_/de'ang cis shes she na/_don gcig ces pa'ang 'bras bu'i tshul gcig pa la bshad cing /_gnas lugs ji lta ba bzhin rtogs pa'i lta ba ni 'bras

[\[32a.3\]]phar phyin theg par sbyin sogs 'khor gsum mi dmigs par spyod pa'i tshul sogs ma rmongs pa'i shes rab bstan pas/_der thabs la ma rmongs pa yod pa gang zhig_/bden pa gnyis dang /_mtshan nyid gsum dang /_phar phyin drug dang /_byang phyogs so bdun sogs de kho na nyid rtogs

[\[32a.5\]]thabs mkhas kyang bstan pas dka' ba med par yang grub/_spros pa'i mtha' brgyad dang bral ba sogs kyi lta ba zab pa dang de la brten pa'i mtshan ma med pa'i spyod pa rab 'byams bstan pa rnams gang zag dbang po ches shin tu rnon po'i dbang du byas par mdo rnams su gsal ba dang /_'dod na zhag bdun 
[\[32a.6\]]gyis kyang 'tshang rgya ba sogs lam myur ba'i tshul yang yod pa sogs mtshungs pa'i phyir ro/_/zhes dogs pa skye srid kyang skyon med de/_khyod kyis bshad pa de lta na ma rmongs pa dang thabs mang ba sogs kyi ming tsam mtshungs par zad kyi/_/lung de las bshad pa'i don ni/_rim pa gnyis dang zung 'jug gi rnal 
[\[32a.7\]]'byor khyad par can dang /_'pho med kyi tshul khrims dang /_/'gyur med lhan skyes kyi bde ba sogs phar phyin theg par ming tsam yang ma grags pa'i khyad par gyi/_zab mo'i gnad gsang 'byam klas pa 'di la yod pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis ma rmongs pa sogs bzhag pa ste de nyid las/_mkhas pa snying rje cher 
[\[32b.1\]]ldan pas/_/dpyad de thabs kyi mchog len cing /_/tha mal pa yi thabs smad nas/_/mi 'pho ba yi gnas 'thob bo/_/zhes sems can mang po la phan gdags par mi nus pa'i mgo la sogs pa sbyin pa sogs tha mal gyi thabs smad nas sems can thams cad kyi re ba cig 
[\[32b.2\]]car du sa skong bar byed pa'i thabs mchog_rim gnyis dang zung 'jug gi ting nge 'dzin gyi 'bras bu khyad par du 'phags pa bsgrubs te myur du mi 'gyur mi 'pho pa'i gnas thob nas lhun grub kyi phrin las 'byung ba thabs la ma rmongs par bshad pa'i phyir dang /_sems can 
[\[32b.3\]]kun don legs bsgrub phyir/_/blo chen la ni thabs thams cad/_/dbye ba rnam bzhir tshul gyi mchog_/'gro ba'i ston pas gsungs pa yin/_/zhes dka' thub dang sdom pa sogs phyogs re ba'i thabs kyis gdul bya mtha' dag rjes su 'dzin par mi nus pas/
[\[32b.4\]]'dir phar phyin drug sogs kyi thabs de yod pa gzhir bzhag nas de'i steng du gdul bya thams cad la rjes su 'gro ba'i thabs dper na dang por rang rig dang lhag lha sogs nges par byas nas 'dod chags che ba'i rigs can gyis 'dod chags rdo rje'i lha sngags phyag rgya ting 
[\[32b.5\]]nge 'dzin bsgom pa sogs mang po gsungs pa dag rgyud sde bzhi'i tshul du bstan pas thabs mang ba yin pa'i phyir dang /_gang zhig gang du ji ltar 'dod/_/de nyid de la nges sbyor zhing /_/'dod pa'i don ni thob mdzad pa'i/_/dam pa'i don ni thub pas gsungs/_/
[\[32b.6\]]zhes nyon mongs pa shas che ba rnams dang por thabs gzhan gyi mgo smad nas rim pas stong pa nyid sgom pa sogs dus ring por goms mi dgos par thog ma nyid nas sems can rnams rang rang gis ji ltar 'dod pa de dang mthun pa'i thabs kyang ston pa/_dper na dbang rnon gyi 
[\[32b.7\]]dbang rtul chags pas shin tu gdungs pa'i skye bo la las rgya/_chags pa de las shas chung ba la dam rgya/_'dod pa'i bag chags kyi rnam rtog ma spangs pa tsam la ye rgya/_dbang rnon gyi dbang rnon gnyis med kyi de kho na nyid la mos pa rnams la phyag chen sogs rang 'dod kyi rjes su 'jug pa'i 
[\[33a.1\]]thabs dang rnal 'byor yod pas dka' ba med par bshad de/_rang gi mos pa bzhin du spyod pa ni dka' ba med par grub pa'i phyir dang /_tshul sgron las/_'dir bden pa'i de kho na nyid kyi rnal 'byor pa ni de kho na nyid kyi thabs ma shes pa'i phyir dbang po 
[\[33a.2\]]rtul po yin par shes par bya'o/_/pha rol tu phyin pa'i de kho na nyid kyi rnal 'byor ni thabs nyid la 'khrul pa yin pa'i phyir dbang po 'bring po yin no/_/gsang sngags kyi sgor spyad pa spyod pa rnams ni gang du'ang rnam par rmongs pa med pas na dbang po rnon po yin no/_/de 
[\[33a.3\]]bas na dbang po rnon po rnams ni gang gzhan dgu byed na ngan 'gror 'gro bar 'gyur ba de nyid kyi phyin ci ma log pa'i thabs la mkhas pas kun tu spyod pa'i sngags kyi brtul zhugs can ni rnam par dag pa'i gnas thob par 'gyur ro zhes sngar bshad pa'i tshul de dag dang ldan pas dbang 
[\[33a.4\]]po rnon po'i dbang du byas par yang 'grub par bshad cing /_phar phyin theg pa'i dbang rnon de la sngags kyi brtul zhugs 'di ma bstan pa'i phyir 'di la ltos nas dbang 'bring du grub pa'i phyir dang /_phar phyin theg par 'dod na zhag bdun gyis 'grub pa'ang sa brgyad pa thob 
[\[33a.5\]]nas yin pa'i phyir/_/de tshun chad myur na'ang grangs med gnyis 'gor bas lam bgrod thog ring la/_'dir de ltar 'gor ba med pa'i phyir ro/_/slob dpon badzra pA Nis kyang /_don de kho na nyid la dbye ba med kyang pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa ni rmongs pa ste/_lung dang 
[\[33a.6\]]rigs pas gtan la phab ste rtogs pa'o/_/rdo rje theg pa ni ma rmongs pa ste/_lung dang /_rigs pa dang /_bla ma'i man ngag gis nyams su myong ba'o/_/gzhan yang dka' ba med pa ste/_bde ba chen po lam du byed pa'o/_/pha rol tu phyin pa ni btang snyoms pa 
[\[33a.7\]]dang nyams su myong ba med pa'o/_/rgyu lam du byed pas na rgyu'i theg pa'o/_/'bras bu lam du byed pas na 'bras bu'i theg pa khyad du 'phags so zhes bkral zhing /_de ltar bkral bas thabs mang ba dang ches dbang po rnon po'i dbang du byas par yang shugs kyis gsal lo/_/
[\[33b.1\]]yang na thabs la mkhas pa rnam pa bcu gcig gis khyad par du 'phags te/_slob dpon dz+nyA na shIs/_gsang sngags kyi theg pa 'di pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa chen po/_dbu ma las kyang khyad par ci yod pa bstan te/_dmigs pa bla na med pa la dmigs pa'i 
[\[33b.2\]]thabs dang /_sgrub pa bla na med pa dang /_ye shes bla na med pa dang /_brtson 'grus bla na med pa dang /_gdul bya ma lus pa 'dzin par nus pa dang /_nyon mongs pa byin gyis rlob pa dang /_byin gyi rlob pa myur ba dang /_myur du 'byung ba dang /_nyon 
[\[33b.3\]]mongs pa spong ba dang /_bsam pa bla na med pa dang /_spyod pa bla na med pa'i thabs mkhas pa ste/_de ltar thabs mkhas pa nyid rnam pa bcu gcig gis khyad par du 'phags so/_/zhes pa ltar ro/_/de dag kyang rim pa bzhin phar phyin theg par ma grags 
[\[33b.4\]]pa'am/_dman pa thams cad la gzhir bzhag nas dgyes rdor 'bum lnga la sogs pa gzhung rgya chen po lam 'dir dmigs pa'i phyir dang /_ting nge 'dzin thob nas mngon sum ma yin pa'i don byed nus pa'i phyir dang /_ting 'dzin khyad par can la bsten pas rgyu 
[\[33b.5\]]dang ngo bo nyid dang las dag las ye shes kyi rgyu shin tu myur ba'i phyir dang /_dam tshig gi dbang gis brtson 'grus chen po rang dbang med par rtsom pa'i phyir dang /_mtshams med byed pa sogs theg pa gzhan las spangs pa rnams kyang lam 'di'i gdul byar gsungs 
[\[33b.6\]]pa'i phyir dang /_nyon mongs pa ma spangs par yul khyad par can du byas nas/_rang bzhin gyis gnas su dag pa'i tshul gyis spong ba'i phyir dang /_mchod pa'i rang bzhin dang bde ba la brten pa'i rdzogs rim gyis nyon mongs pa byin gyis rlob pa'i phyir dang /
[\[33b.7\]]de bzhin gshegs pas dbang bskur ba/_/sa la zhugs nas thob par 'gyur/_/zhes pa lta bu ma yin par da lta nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis byin gyis rlob pa'i phyir dang /_zung 'jug gi go 'phang tshe gcig nyid la thob pa sogs 'di la yod pa'i phyir 
[\[34a.1\]]dang /_sangs rgyas rnams kyi sku lha sgom pa dang /_gsung sngags bzla ba dang /_thugs ting nge 'dzin sgom pa ste sbyor ba gsum dang ldan pa'i phyir dang /_mi mthun pa'i spyod pa gsum ste/_nus pa dman pa'i spyod pa phyi rol gyi dka' thub sdom pa 
[\[34a.2\]]sogs dang /_g.yeng byed kyi spyod pa de bzhin nyid la brtan pa ma thob par rtsol ba'i lus ngag gi dge sbyor sogs dang /_dngos 'dzin gyi spyod pa gtsang sme'i rtog pa sogs te/_de rnams las bzlog pa'i spyod pa/_dka' thub sdom pa mi bzad pa/_/bsten pas 
[\[34a.3\]]'grub par mi 'gyur gyi/_/'dod pa'i longs spyod thams cad la/_/brten nas myur du 'grub par 'gyur/_/zhes sogs dang /_gal te byang chub mchog 'dod na/_/glegs bam bklag par mi bya zhing /_/mchod rten bskor ba mi bya'o/_/byas na byang

[\[34a.7\]]nyon mongs pa rags pa gcod pa'i dbang thob pa na bya ba pa phyi rol pa spyad pa'am/_yang na sems stong pa nyid 'ba' zhig bsgom pas chog gi lus dang*ngag gi bya ba mi dgos te/_rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa las/_mtshan mar bcas pas mtshan bcas

[\[34b.4\]]yang slob dpon DoM bi pas/_'di ni snod kyi khyad par dang /_/snod du byed pa'i chos dang ni/_/gzhung dang lam gyi khyad par dang /_/'bras bu dag gi khyad par gyis/_/sngags kyi theg pa khyad par 'phags/_/zhes gsungs pa sogs khyad par 'byed pa'i tshul

[\[34b.6\]]mo/_/zhes dang /_in+d+ra b+hU tis/_bla ma'i khyad par dang /_snod kyi khyad par dang /_cho ga'i khyad par dang /_las kyi khyad par dang /_dam tshig gi khyad par dang /_lta ba'i khyad par dang /_spyod pa'i khyad par te bdun gyis 'phags so/_/zhes sogs 
[\[34b.7\]]kyi lung gis lta ba dang 'bras bu gnyis car la khyad zhugs par bzhed cing /_'chad tshul 'di la rdo rje theg pa'i gnad gsang khyad par ba mang du yod par snang yang /_re zhig yongs grags ltar byas pa'o/_/gnyis pa dbye ba'i tshul la/_slob dpon a ti shas/_/

[\[37a.3\]]ma'i rgyud bstan to/_/zhes spang bya nyon mongs pa'i sgo nas dang /_nag po zhabs kyis/_dus ni rnam bzhi dbye ba las/_/rgyud ni rnam pa bzhir 'gyur te/_/zhes dang /_dri med 'od las/_'dir thun dang po'i mngon mtshams la rgod pa'i rgyud do/_/thun

[\[37a.7\]]pa'i rigs dang /_pad+ma'i rigs/_rdo rje'i rigs/_nor bu'i rigs/_rgyas pa'i rigs/_'jig rten pa'i rigs rnams kyi rgyud drug yod pa'i phyir ro/_/de re re la rigs kyi gtso bo/_rigs kyi bdag po/_rigs kyi yum/_rigs kyi gtsug 
[\[37b.1\]]tor/_rigs kyi khro bo/_rigs kyi khro mo/_rigs kyi pho nya/_rigs kyi pho nya mo/_rigs kyi bka' nyan/_rigs kyi bka' nyan ma rnams ci rigs par 'dus pa'am/_re re nas brjod bya'i gtso bor byas pa'i sgo nas dbyer yod do/_/de dag nye bar

[\[38a.1\]]ba'i rigs lnga'i dbye bas rgyud kyang lnga dang zhib mor phye bas brgyar yang 'gyur te/_rdo rje rtse mor/_rigs ni rnam pa du yin brjod/_/rigs ni rnam pa brgyar gsungs te/_/mdo ru bsdu na rnam pa lnga/_/sangs rgyas rdo rje rin chen dang /_/chos dang

[\[41b.3\]]rten pa'i lha la sogs pas smras pa/_ston pas byin gyis brlabs pa sogs ci rigs par yod do/_/spyod pa'i rgyud kyang gtso bor 'og min chen po dang /_sum cu rtsa gsum sogs su bstan pa ste phal cher bya ba'i rgyud dang phyogs mtshungs so/_/rnal 'byor rgyud 
[\[41b.4\]]ni ston pa 'og min du longs spyod rdzogs skur sangs rgyas nas/_longs sku chung ngu'am/_sprul sku'i rnam snang ri rab kyi rtse mor gshegs nas/_de bzhin gshegs pa'i dkyil 'khor chen por sprul bshad mdzad pa'i tshul gyis gtso bor gsungs shing /_gzhan 
[\[41b.5\]]ni gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi gnas sogs su ma nges par bstan par mdzad do/_/rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i rgyud ni 'og min dang /_dga' ldan dang /_ri rab kyi rtse dang /_o rgyan dang /_dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi mchod rten la sogs pa gnas kyi bye brag

[\[73a.2\]]u rgya u pA si ka zhes pa zhig gis de'i sgrub g.yog byas pas/_ro'i lus gser du gyur pa thob pa'i gser la brten te/_ma ga d+hA'i phyogs gcig tu o tan+ta pu ri'i gtsug lag khang ri rab gling bzhi'i tshul du bzhengs/_dge slong lnga brgya dang dge

[\[87b.1\]]gtugs shing /_khyad par bal po'i 'dul 'dzin sbe ta ka las 'dul ba'i lag len thams cad la mkhas par sbyangs/_kha che dz+hA na shi las so thar mdo'i 'grel pa 'dul ba bsdus pa dang /_kha che thi su b+hU ti shAn+ta las sum brgya ba rtsa 'grel/_sa man+ta shrI dz+nyA na las kA ri ka lnga bcu ba dang lo

[\[91a.7\]]man ngag sogs ci rigs par snang ngo*/_/bstan pa phyi dar gyi tshe bya ba'i rgyud dang spyod pa'i rgyud gnyis la brten pa'i dbang bka' dang /_rjes gnang dang /_rig gtad tsam dang lung sbyin pa sogs las 'chad nyan gyi srol ni ma byung bar mngon la/_bla ma kha cig gis dpung bzang 
[\[91b.1\]]sogs la bshad pa byas par grags pa'ang rtsal bshad byas pa nyid du zad kyi bshad rgyun 'ded rgyu yod pa ma mthong ngo /_/rnal 'byor rgyud ni lo chen rin chen bzang po kha cher byon te bla ma mang po bsten/_rgyud dang gdams ngag mang po nyan nas/_gsang sngags spyi dang khyad

[\[91b.3\]]len nges tig mdzad de/_rngog legs she sogs thugs sras bzhi gtso bor gyur pa'i slob ma mang po la gnang ste/_'chad nyan gyis brgyud pa zin pa shin tu mang bar byung /_de las pho brang zhi ba 'od kyis paN+Di ta man+tA ka lA sha sogs spyan drangs te/_'gyur mang du

[\[92a.1\]]te bsgyur bshad ci rigs par mdzad mod kyi gtso bor mar 'gos kyi lugs gnyis su grags che/_de'ang 'gos lugs ni lo tsA ba chen po 'gos zhug pa lha btsas kyis slob dpon chen po dI paM ka ra dang /_de wA ka ra tsan+dA dang /_bir+ya b+ha dra sogs paN+Di ta bdun cu/_mkha' 'gro ma

[\[92a.7\]]dang /_dpyal chos kyi bzang po sogs la gnang ba nas paN chen lugs su grags pa'ang byung ngo*/_/gzhan yang bshad srol cung zad 'dra min yod pa'i rgyun sna tshogs zhig byung 'dug kyang bris pas mi lang ngo*/_/phyi ma ye shes zhabs lugs ni dang por lo chen rin bzang las rkyang

[\[92b.7\]]las/_snga ma ni gshed dmar gyi skor te dpyal lo chos dpal bzang pos niSh+ka lang+ka la zhus nas bod du dar ba dang /_dA na shI las sa skya paN chen la gnang ba dang /_chag los kyang birU pa'i gzhung sogs bsgyur cing bstan pa dang /_glo bo lo tsAs 
[\[93a.1\]]darba na A tsAr+ya sogs las gsan cing spel ba rnams te/_de dag gi rgyun las/_gshed dmar gyi skor rnams kyi dbang khrid man ngag dang bcas pa byung ba yin no/_/rwa lugs ni/_rwa lo rdo rje grags kyi bal po 'ba' ro phyag

[\[93a.6\]]ra dang /_'brog mi dpon slob sogs kyis bsgyur bshad mdzad pa dang /_mar 'gos gnyis kyis bshad sgrub kyi srol cher btod pa yin no/_/sgyu 'phrul chen mo'ang de dang mtshungs shing /_sangs rgyas thod pa la gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer sogs kyis rgyud 
[\[93a.7\]]'grel bsgyur bshad mdzad pa dang /_mar 'gos sogs las kyang dar ro/_/bde mchog gi skor ni/_phyi dar gyi thog mar jo bo rjes lo chen rin bzang dang /_rong pa mgar dge sogs la gnang zhing /_paN+Di ta mang po la bsten nas lo chen dang /_'gos 
[\[93b.1\]]sogs kyis rgyud dang /_sgrub thabs/_'grel pa sogs bde mchog skor gyi gzhung mang du bsgyur/_phyis jo bos nag tsho lo tsA sogs la'ang gnang ba nas dar ba dang /_glog skya shes rab brtsegs kyis/_/bal por pham thing pa sku mched la bde mchog

[\[96a.1\]]la/_kawa mi tra/_dzi na mi tra/_su ren+d+ra bod+hi/_shrI len+d+ra bod+hi/_dA na shI la/_bod+hi mi tra/_mu ni warma/_sarba dz+nya de wa/_di n+ya pra b+ha sogs dang /_rgya'i slob dpon hwa shang ma hA de ba tshe/_hA shang ma ko se/_hA shang ma hA ya na sogs

[\[102a.1\]]dkar chen byang chub 'bum gyi sras/_bde chen bsod nams bzang po zhes pa yum 'das pa'i dgongs rdzogs bsgrub par/_kathog rdo rje gdan du byon nas phyir ma log pas/_mched gzhan gyis slar 'gugs par btang rtsis

[\[136b.2\]]mkhan po a dzi ta shrI b+ha dra dang /_lo tsA ba seng dkar dge slong shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/_mig bcu gnyis pa zhes bya ba'i mdo 'gyur byang med pa rnams bzhugs so//_//gsang sngags rgyud 'bum du grags pa'i

[\[136b.4\]]rgyud/_rnal 'byor gyi rgyud/_spyod pa'i rgyud bya ba'i rgyud de rtsa ba'i sa bcad bzhi dang /_mthar phun sum tshogs pa'i yan lag tu bsngo smon shis brjod kyi skor ro/_/dang po bla med rgyud la/_gong smos ltar pha ma'i rgyud gnyis las gnyis med

[\[137a.3\]]sngags kyi theg pa mi shes pa de dag thams cad ni 'khor ba pa ste bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa'i lam dang bral ba'o/_/zhes rgyud thams cad kyi dngos don mthar thug yin pa dang /_khyad par dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud rnams kyi snying por gyur pa gsal

[\[137a.5\]]che'i paN+Di ta so ma nA tha dang /_lo tsA ba 'bro dge slong shes rab grags kyis bsgyur cing /_slar yang sgra tshad pa rin chen rgyal mtshan gyis dpal nA ro pa'i 'grel bshad dang mthun par bsgyur cing zhus pa/_mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas las phyung

[\[137a.7\]]gnyis la gtugs shing zhus pa/_'di la phyis 'gyur bcos mdzad pa po'ang mang zhig byung mod kyi shong 'gyur nyid don bzang bar mkhas pa rnams la grags pa yin no/_/dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud phyi ma rgyud kyi snying po zhes bya ba/_shAkya'i dge

[\[138a.1\]]bsdus pa bde mchog nyung ngu'i rgyud yin te/_'di la le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig_/sh+lo ka stong bdun brgya ba paN+Di ta pad+ma ka ra dang /_lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur la/_sgra bsgyur dge slong pra dz+hA kIrti dang mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug

[\[138a.7\]]sdom pa 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po le'u so gsum pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po gzhan phan mtha' yas dang /_lo tsA ba rgyus brje smon lam grags kyis bsgyur cing /_slar yang paN+Di ta chen po shrI ba na rit+ta'i rgya dpe la gtugs nas lo tsA

[\[138b.2\]]'bar gyis bsgyur cing zhus pa/_rnal 'byor ma kun tu spyod pa'i rgyud le'u bcu bdun pa/_lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus pa/_rnal 'byor ma bzhi'i kha sbyor ba'i rgyud brtag pa bdun pa/_lo tsA ba chings yon tan 'bar gyi 'gyur/
[\[138b.3\]]phag mo mngon par brjod pa bshad pa'i rgyud phyi ma las phag mo mngon par byang chub pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po tsA nA ka ra'i zhal snga nas lo tsA ba khu dngos grub kyis bsgyur ba/_mkha' 'gro ma thams cad kyi thugs gnyis su med pa'i ye shes bsam

[\[138b.7\]]pa ga ya d+ha ra'i zhal snga nas dang lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur te 'di'i rtsa rgyud rgyas pa sum cu rtsa drug yod par in+d+ra b+hU ti'i 'grel pa las 'byung zhing /_rtsa rgyud bsdus pa 'di la sh+lo ka nyis stong brgya bdun cu don lnga/_rgyud phyi ma la drug brgya nyi shu rtsa brgyad dang

[\[141a.1\]]bcas pa/_/rdo rje'i tshig mang ldan pa 'dir/_/zhes pa ltar ro/_/brtag gnyis la ltos nas bshad rgyud dang /_'bum lngar ltos nas bsdus rgyud du bzhed pa/_mkha' 'gro ma dra ba rdo rje gur zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u bco lnga ba/_rgya gar gyi 
[\[141a.2\]]mkhan po ga ya d+ha ra dang 'brog mi'i 'gyur/_rgyud phyi ma phyag rgya chen po thig le zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor ma chen mo'i rgyud kyi rgyal po'i mnga' bdag le'u nyi shu rtsa brgyad pa/_slob dpon chen po dpal shes rab gsang ba'i zhal snga nas/_kam chos kyi ye shes dang /
[\[141a.3\]]phyug mtshams dgra bcom gyis bsgyur ba/_rgyud phyi ma'i yang phyi ma dpal ye shes snying po zhes bya ba rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u bzhi ba/_paN+Di ta shes rab gsang ba'i rang 'gyur/_bshad pa'i rgyud dpal ye shes thig le rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal 
[\[141a.4\]]po mchog tu rmad du byung ba le'u sum cu pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI pra dz+nyA gu pas bsgyur cing /_slad kyis dpal sa skyar zhu tig bgyis pa/_'bras bu'i rgyud dpal de kho na nyid kyi sgron ma rnal 'byor chen mo'i rgyud kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba 'gyur snga ma dang 'dra ba rnams so/_/
[\[141a.5\]]gsum pa sangs rgyas thod pa'i skor la rtsa ba'i rgyud stong phrag bcu gnyis pa las phyung ba'i dpal sangs rgyas thod pa zhes bya ba rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u bcu bzhi ba/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI ga ya d+ha ra dang /_lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba 'di kho na'o/_/
[\[141a.6\]]bzhi ba ma hA mA yA'i skor la/_sgyu 'phrul chen mo zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u gsum pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na pa ra dang /_lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyis bsgyur cing slar yang glog skya shes rab brtsegs kyis bsgyur ba nyid do/_/lnga ba A ra li'i skor la/_rdo rje A ra 
[\[141a.7\]]li'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u dgu ba/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po kA yas+thA pa ga ya d+ha ra'i zhal snga nas dang /_lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/_ri gi A ra li'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u lnga pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po ga ya d+ha ra dang /_lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyis bsgyur ba dag 
[\[141b.1\]]go/_/gsum pa rnam snang gi rigs kyi rgyud la gdan bzhi rtsa ba'i rgyud rgyas pa stong phrag sum cu rtsa gnyis pa las bsdus pa'i dpal gdan bzhi ba zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po gser gyi char par grags pa gdan bzhi po re rer rab byed bzhi bzhi yod pas 
[\[141b.2\]]rab byed bcu drug pa dang /_de'i bshad pa'i rgyud sngags kyi cha zhes bya ba le'u brgyad pa gnyis rgya gar gyi mkhan po ga ya d+ha ra dang lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/_dpal gdan bzhi ba'i rnam par bshad pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po rnal 'byor ma thams cad gsang ba zhes 
[\[141b.3\]]bya ba le'u brgya lhag pa/_paN+Di ta spyi ti dz+nyA na kIrtis gsar du bsgyur ba/_mi g.yo ba'i rgyud dpal gtum po khro bo chen po'i rgyud kyi rgyal po dpa' bo gcig pa zhes bya ba lus kyi rim par phye la sogs pas rab tu phye ba'i le'u nyi shu rtsa lnga ba/_paN+Di ta rat+na shrI'i zhal snga 
[\[141b.4\]]nas/_lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis dpal sa skyar bsgyur ba bzhugs so/_/ca pa la/'phags pa mi g.yo ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po 'bum pa las byung ba dngos grub thams cad yongs su 'byung ba'i rtog pa le'u bdun/_paN+Di ta a tu la dA sa badzra dang /
[\[141b.5\]]lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug grags pa'i 'gyur/_khro bo'i rgyal po thams cad gsang sngags gsang ba'i rgyud le'u lnga ba dang /_mi g.yo ba gsang ba'i rgyud chen po le'u bzhi ba gnyis la 'gyur byang ma 'khod pa rnams so/_/bzhi pa rdo rje nyi ma'i rigs kyi rgyud 
[\[141b.6\]]ni/_rdo rje bdud rtsi'i rgyud kyi rgyal po stong phrag bcu gnyis pa las bsdus pa rdo rje bdud rtsi nyung ngu'i rgyud le'u bcu gcig pa/_lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba nyid do/_/lnga ba pad+ma gar dbang gi rigs kyi rgyud la/_dpal pad+ma 'bar ba'i rgyud 
[\[141b.7\]]chen po las phyung ba/_rigs kyi 'jig rten mgon po lnga bcu ba le'u gsum/_paN+Di ta bi ma la shrI b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas/_lo tsA ba shud ke grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba/_'phags ma sgrol ma ku ru kul+le'i rtog pa le'u lnga/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po 
[\[142a.1\]]kr-iShA paN+Di ta dang*lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur ro/_drug pa rta mchog gi rigs kyi rgyud la/_/sgrol ma phyag 'tshal nyi shu rtsa gcig gi bstod pa phan yon dang bcas pa 'gyur byang ma 'khod pa ste/_/'di slob dpon nyi ma sbas pas bla med 
[\[142a.2\]]du bkral ba ltar 'dir bkod/_rdo rje phur pa rtsa ba'i rgyud biTot+ta ma 'bum sde'i dum bu slob dpon pad+ma 'byung gnas kyi rgya dpe dang mthun par dpal sa skya paN+Di tas bsgyur ba/_nag po chen po mgon po mngon pa 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u lnga bcu 
[\[142a.3\]]ba/_paN+Di ta chen po sa man+ta b+hi dang /_lo tsA ba rwa chos rab kyi 'gyur rnams so/_/bdun pa rigs drug pa khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang gi rgyud ni/_ji bzhin brnyes pa nam mkha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud le'u lnga pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po tA k+Sha ka ga Na dang /
[\[142a.4\]]lo tsA ba mang 'or byang chub shes rab kyi 'gyur nyid do/_/gsum pa thabs gtso bor ston pa pha'i rgyud la/_mi bskyod pa/_rnam snang /_rin 'byung /_'od dpag med/_don yod grub pa/_drug pa rdo rje 'chang gi rigs gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud de 
[\[142a.5\]]drug yod do/_/dang po la/_gsang 'dus kyi rtsa rgyud chen mo la ltos nas nyung ngu'i rtsa ba'i rgyud du grags pa/_/de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs kyi gsang chen gsang ba 'dus pa zhes bya ba'i brtag pa'i rgyal po la le'u bcu 
[\[142a.6\]]bdun dang /_de'i rgyud phyi ma le'u gcig pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsAr+ya shAng+d+hA ka ra warma dang /_lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/_gsang 'dus bshad rgyud dgongs pa lung bstan pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud le'u bcu gnyis pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma shrI 
[\[142a.7\]]b+ha dra dang /_lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/_rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud thams cad kyi snying po gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad rgyud rdo rje phreng ba le'u drug cu rtsa brgyad/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po su dza na shrI dang /_lo tsA ba bod kyi lha btsan po bla ma dge slong zhi ba'i 
[\[142b.1\]]'od kyi zhal snga nas bsgyur cing zhus pa/_lha mo bzhis yongs su zhus pa le'u bzhi/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po spro ti dz+nyA na kIrti'i rang 'gyur/_ye shes rdo rje kun las btus pa'i rgyud las le'u gnyis logs su bkol ba/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po tsA nA ka ra'i zhal snga 
[\[142b.2\]]nas dang /_lo tsA ba khu dngos grub kyi 'gyur la/_slad nas nag tsho lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas zhus shing gtan la phab pa rnams bzhugs so/_/dpal ye shes rdo rje kun las btus pa rab byed bzhi bcu rtsa gcig pa/_kha che'i paN+Di ta A ka ra 
[\[142b.3\]]sid+d+hi dang /_lo tsA ba nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/_rdo rje snying po rgyan gyi rgyud le'u bcu bdun pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la gup+ta dang /_lo tsA ba lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/_dpal gnyis su med pa rnam par rgyal ba'i ngo bo nyid kyi rdo rje 
[\[142b.4\]]zhes bya ba le'u nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa/_mkhan chen thar pa lo tsA ba'i phyag dpa'i khrod nas shog yar lnga byung ba sngar bsgyur ba las/_phyis nyang stod smon 'gro'i gtsug lag khang nas rgya dpe lhag ma rnams rnyed pa las/_bu ston gyis rdzogs par bsgyur ba/_dpal 
[\[142b.5\]]de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba rnal 'byor chen po rnams par rgyal ba zhes bya ba nyam pa nyid gnyis su med pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po rdo rje dpal mchog chen po brtag pa dang po la le'u bdun cu rtsa bdun/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal ye shes snying po dang /
[\[142b.6\]]lo tsA ba lho brag mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus pa rnams bzhugs so/_/gnyis med rnam rgyal chen mo 'di la chag lo ba sogs kyis rgyud yang dag pa ma yin par mdzad mod kyi/_nA ro 'grel chen du gnyis med rnam rgyal gyi lung drangs rnams kyang 
[\[142b.7\]]'di dang 'gyur khyad tsam ma gtogs don la khyad ma zhugs pa dang /_'di'i bskyed rdzogs kyi rnam gzhag rnams kyang rtsa rgyud kyi rnam gzhag dang mthun pa dang /_paN+Di ta chen po smra \u0f80ti dz+nyA na kIrti'i rang 'gyur zhig kyang yod par bshad pa dang /_gsang ba 'dus pa la 
[\[143a.1\]]mkhas pa khams pa ro mnyam rdo rje'i TI ka sogs la'ang 'di tshad mar byas so/_ja ba la/_'phags pa lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can drag po gsum 'dul zhes bya ba'i rtsa rgyud/_paN+Di ta de wa pUr+Na ma ti dang lo tsA ba 'gar chos kyi bzang 
[\[143a.2\]]po'i 'gyur/_gos sngon po can gyi bshad rgyud drag po gsum 'dul zhes bya ba le'u gsum pa 'gyur byang snga ma dang 'dra ba/_lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi cho ga rdo rje be con gyi rgyud le'u bco lnga ba 'gyur byang ma 'khod pa/_lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can 
[\[143a.3\]]rdo rje gdengs pa'i rgyud khams gsum las rnam par rgyal ba zhes bya ba le'u gcig pa paN+Di ta a Da ya shrI ma ti dang /_lo tsA ba ban+de chos kyi dbang phyug grags kyi 'gyur/_dpal rdo rje gtum po thugs gsang ba'i rgyud dpal gtum po zhes bya ba 
[\[143a.4\]]le'u nyi shu rtsa bzhi pa dang /_dpal rdo rje gtum po thugs gsang ba'i rgyud phyi ma le'u bcu bzhi ba dang /_dpal rdo rje gtum po thugs gsang ba'i rgyud phyi ma'i phyi ma le'u brgyad pa rnams rgya gar gyi mkhan po a ba yuk+ti dang /_lo tsA ba bla ban chos 
[\[143a.5\]]kyi brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/_lag na rdo rje'i rmi lam mthong ba 'gyur byang med pa/_phyag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gnod sbyin drag po rdo rje me lce'i rgyud le'u bco lnga pa/_paN+Di ta rat+na kIrti dang lo tsA ba dge tshul khyung drags kyi 'gyur/_rdo rje snying po lce dbab 
[\[143a.6\]]pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs dang po ska cog gi 'gyur la/_phyis gnyan lo dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/_/dpal phyag na rdo rje gsang ba bstan pa'i rgyud le'u bdun pa/_paN+Di ta ba la tsan+d+ra dang /_lo tsA ba glan chung dar ma tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/_bcom ldan 
[\[143a.7\]]'das phyag na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u nyi shu rtsa gcig pa/_paN+Di ta wa la tsan+d+ra dang /_lo tsA ba glan chung dar ma tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/_rdo rje bde khros kyi rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u bcu bdun pa dz+hA nA ka ra'i 'gyur rnams so/_/
[\[143b.1\]]gnyis pa rnam snang gi rigs su gtogs pa'i rgyud la/_rgyud kyi rgyal po rnam par snang mdzad sgyu 'phrul dra ba zhes bya ba le'u bcu ba lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/_rnam snang gi rigs kyi khro bo'i skor la/_de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku 
[\[143b.2\]]gsung thugs gshin rje gshed nag po zhes bya ba'i rgyud le'u bco brgyad pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang /_lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur la/_slad kyi lo tsA ba dar ma grags kyis bcos pa/_slar yang rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta bA ro phyag 
[\[143b.3\]]rdum gyi zhal snga nas dang /_lo tsA ba rdo rje grags kyis gtan la phab pa/_dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed dngos grub grub pa'i rgyud rtog pa bdun pa/_dpal o rgyun gyi gnas nas 'jam dpal gyi rgyud las dpal la li ta badzras phyung ste spyan drangs pa/
[\[143b.4\]]paN+Di ta bA ro phyag rdum dang /_lo tsA ba rdo rje grags kyi 'gyur/_gshin rje gshed nag po'i rgyud kyi rgyal po rtog pa gsum pa 'gyur byang ma 'khod kyang paN+Di ta a Da ya shrI dang rong zom gyis bsgyur bar grags pa/_dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi dngos 
[\[143b.5\]]grub kyi rtog pa zhes bya ba le'u bzhi ste rtog pa bzhi bar grags pa/_paN+Di ta a mo g+ha'i zhabs dang /_lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug grags pa'i 'gyur la/_slad kyis grub thob kaN shrI'i zhal snga nas thar pa lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing 
[\[143b.6\]]bcos pa/_gtam rgyud kyi rtog pa 'gyur byang ma 'khod kyang dI paM ka ra dang rwa lo'i 'gyur/_las mkhan te'u lo pa chu bya'i rtog pa 'gyur byang snga ma dang 'dra ba/_gshin rje gshed nag po'i las thams cad grub par byed pa'i 'khor lo'i rgyud kyi rgyal 
[\[143b.7\]]po paN+Di ta bA ro phyag rdum gyi zhal snga nas rwa rdo rje grags kyis bsgyur ba/_dpal gshin rje'i gshed dmar po zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u bcu dgu ba shAkya'i dge slong tsan+d+ra shri'i zhal snga nas zhus shing /_/paN+Di ta chen po tsan+d+ra kIrti dang /_yar 
[\[144a.1\]]lungs pa grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bal po yam bu'i grong khyer du bsgyur ba/_dpal gshin rje'i gshed dmar po'i rgyud le'u nyer gnyis pa skad gnyis smra ba chen po thar pa lo tsAs bskyangs pa/_lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur 
[\[144a.2\]]rnams so/_/gsum pa rin po che'i rigs kyi rgyud bod du 'gyur ba ma rnyed ces bu ston gsung ngo /_bzhi ba pad+ma'i rigs kyi rgyud la/_dpal bcom ldan 'das ral pa gcig pa'i brtag pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po paN+Di ta dza ga tra mi tra A nan+da'i bka' 
[\[144a.3\]]drin las/_rgya gar nub phyogs kyi paN+Di ta badzra shrI kha la ru dra dang /_lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur ro/_/lnga ba las kyi rigs kyi rgyud kyang mi bzhugs so/_drug pa rdo rje 'chang gi rigs kyi rgyud la/_dpal zla gsang thig le zhes bya ba'i 
[\[144a.4\]]rgyud kyi rgyal po shin tu dgyes pa rdo rje gdon mi za ba'i dam tshig gi dkyil 'khor chen po rgyas pa mchog tu gsang ba'i rgyud dge slong rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so/_rtsa ba'i sa bcad gnyis pa rnal 'byor kyi rgyud la thabs gtso bor ston 
[\[144a.5\]]pa'i rgyud dang /_shes rab gtso bor stan pa'i rgyud gnyis/_dang po la rtsa bshad cha mthun gyi rgyud gsum las dang po ni glegs bam nya pa la/_de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi de kho na nyid bsdus pa rtsa ba'i rgyud dum bu bzhi rgyud phyi ma/_phyi 
[\[144a.6\]]ma'i phyi ma rgyud nye bar bsdu ba dang bcas pa bam po dgu lhag pa paN+Di ti shad+hA ka ra warma dang /_lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur bar grags pa'o/_/gnyis pa ni yo ga bshad pa'i rgyud rdo rje rtse mo rtog pa bcu ba las rdo rje mtshan brgyas gsol ba btab 
[\[144a.7\]]pa yan chad rtog pa phyed dang drug yod pa bam po bcu gnyis pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po karma badzra dang lo tsA ba dge slong gzhon nu tshul khrims kyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so/_ta pa la thams cad gsang ba zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma 
[\[144b.1\]]ka ra warma dang /_lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/_'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i rtog pa'i rgyal po rtsa ba'i rgyud phyi ma dang bcas pa kha cig gis rin chen bzang pos sgyur bar bzhed cing /_kha cig gis rma dge blos bsgyur bar bzhed 
[\[144b.2\]]pa la/_mkhas pa zha lu pa ye shes rgya mtshos tshig don la legs par dpyad nas zhus pa rnams so/_gsum pa ni/_de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba gzi 
[\[144b.3\]]brjid kyi rgyal po'i rtog pa zhes bya ba bam po gsum pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAn+ti gab+ha dang /_lo tsA ba ban+de dza ya rak+Shi tas bsgyur ba/_de'i gsham du mngon spyod kyi las 'gyur byang snga ma dang 'dra ba/_ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i 
[\[144b.4\]]snying po'i gzungs/_de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba gzi brjid kyi rgyal po'i rtag pa phyogs gcig pa/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po bla ma rje btsun chen po re ban+de de 
[\[144b.5\]]ba'i zhabs dang /_paN chen mA Ni ka shrI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas chag lo tsA ba chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur ba/_rab tu gnas pa mdor bsdus pa'i rgyud/_kha che'i paN+Di ti dz+nyA na badzra dang /_lo tsA ba 'bro shes rab grags kyi 'gyur rnams so/_/
[\[144b.6\]]gnyis pa shes rab gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud la/_de nyid bsdus pa'i cha mthun gyi rgyud dpal mchog dang po zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i rtog pa'i rgyal po las dum bu dang po shes phyin gyi dum bu/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsAr+ya thud+d+hA ka ra warma dang lo tsA ba 
[\[144b.7\]]rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/_dpal mchog dang po'i dum bu gnyis pa rtsa ba'i rgyud/_rgyud phyi ma dum bu dang po dang gnyis pa'i rtog pa thams cad bsdus pa'i rgyud dum bu gnyis pa nyid kyi rtog pa thams cad kyi rgyud phyi ma'i rtsa ba'i rgyud dang /
[\[145a.1\]]gsang ba ras bris kyi cho ga dang /_/phyag rgya'i rgyud/_rtog pa thams cad kyi rgyud/_phyi ma'i rtsa ba'i rtog pa dang /_rtog pa thams cad sgrub pa'i cho ga dang /_phyag rgya'i rgyud thams cad kyi don gtan la 'bebs pa rtog pa thams cad 
[\[145a.2\]]bsdus pa'i mchog tu gsang ba'i cho ga dang rgyud nye bar sdud pa dang bcas pa rnams paN+Di ta maN+Da ka lA sha dang lo tsA ba lha btsad po zhi ba 'od kyis bsgyur ba/_'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul brgya lnga bcu ba 'gyur byang ma 'khod pa rnams 
[\[145a.3\]]bzhugs te 'di ni mdo phyogs shes phyin skor du bkod zin na'ang /_dpal mchog sher dum dang mtshungs shing sngags su bkral ba'ang yod pa'i phyir 'dir yang bzhag go/_/tha pa la/_dpal rdo rje snying po rgyan ces bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po 
[\[145a.4\]]paN+Di ta su ga ta shrI dang /_chos kyi rje sa skya paN+Di tas ma 'dres pa'i chos bco brgyad kyi skabs thugs kyi phrin las ya thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro ste ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ngo zhes pa'i bar bsgyur ba'i 'phro dpang lo tsA ba dpal ldan blo gros brtan 
[\[145a.5\]]pas rdzogs par bsgyur ba/_'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgo nyi shu rtsa lnga ba zhes bya ba'i mdo 'gyur byang ma 'khod pa/_'di'ang sher phyogs skor phyogs gcig tu bya ba'i phyir shes phyin gras su'ang bzhag mod kyi/_rdo rje snying po rgyan gyi 
[\[145a.6\]]rgyud las byung ba'i sgo nyer lnga ba dang mtshungs pas 'dir yang bcug go/_/de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs gsang ba rgyan gyi bkod pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po bde bar gshegs pa'i dpal dang /_sgra bsgyur ba 
[\[145a.7\]]kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyis dpal sa skyar bsgyur ba/_'phags pa gsang ba nor bu'i thig le zhes bya ba'i rgyud 'gyur byang snga ma dang 'dra ba rnams so/_rtsa ba'i sa bcad gsum pa spyod pa'i rgyud la rigs gsum las/_dang po de bzhin gshegs

[\[155a.2\]]mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gsang sngags dang bcas pa 'gyur byang ma 'khod pa/_'di la bla ma dag rgyud gzhan zhig nas phyung ba yin pa 'dra'o zhes gsungs/_lag na rdo rje'i snying po brgyad kyi ya gyal rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/_rgya gar 
[\[155a.3\]]gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang /_dA na shI la dang /_lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde'i 'gyur/_de'i bshad rgyud rdo rje ri rab chen po'i rtse mo'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i gzungs/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang /_dz+nya na sid+d+hi dang /_lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes

[\[160a.5\]]bu'i gling gi sems can de dag 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la 'jog cing /_bzhag nas kyang lha'i lo stong du yo byad thams cad kyis mi brel bar rjed cing mchod pa bas/_gang gis chos kyi rnam grangs 'di las tshig bzhi ba'i tshigs su bcad pa tsam yang nyan 
[\[160a.6\]]pa dang /_'chang ba dang /_'dri ba dang /_'drir bcug pa dang /_gzhan la rgyas par byed na de bas 'di ches bsod nams mang du 'phel lo/_/zhes gsungs pa dang /_byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bstan pa'i mdo las/_'jam dpal byang chub sems 
[\[160a.7\]]dpa' gang gis bskal pa 'bum gyi bar du thabs la mkhas pa med par pha rol du phyin pa drug la spyad pa bas/_gang gis chos kyi rnam grangs 'di som nyi dang bcas pas thos na 'di ni de bas ches bsod nams mang du skyed na gang gis som nyi med par thos pa lta ci smos/_gang 
[\[160b.1\]]gis yi ger 'dri ba dang /_lung nod pa dang /_'chang ba dang /_gzhan dag la'ang rgya cher yang dag par ston pa lta ci smos/_zhes dang /_de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po zhes bya ba'i mdo las kyang kun dga' bo byang chub sems dpa' gang chos kyi rnam grangs 'di 'chang 
[\[160b.2\]]ba dang /_klog pa dang /_gzhan dag la'ang rgya cher yang dag par rab tu ston pa dang /_glegs bam du byas te 'chang ba des 'di snyam du bdag gis deng nyid bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob bo snyam du sems bskyed par bya ste/_de ni ji ltar da ltar nga bzhin du 
[\[160b.3\]]lha dang mi dang lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis phyag bya ba'i 'os dang /_mchod pa'i 'os yin no/_/zhes 'byung ba sogs mdor na mdo sde re re 'bri ba la'ang de lta bu'i phan yon yod na/_mdo rgyud kyi glegs bam mang po'i phyi mo mi zad pa'i chos sbyin spel ba'i phyir par du

[\[160b.6\]]'khrul ba med pa dpyad pa gsum gyis rnam par dag pa las byung ba yin pa'i phyir sems can gyi bde skyid dang sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa gnyi ga'i rtsa lag tu gyur pa 'di lta bu la ni bsod nams bya ba'i dngos po gang gis kyang bskrun par mi nus pa'i phyir ro/_/khyad par du deng sang 
[\[160b.7\]]snyigs ma lnga bdo ba'i mun klong stug por g.yo bas mnyam med shAkya'i dbang po'i bstan pa rin po che'ang nub pa la thag mi ring ba'i skabs 'di lta bur dam pa'i chos yun ring du gnas pa'i phyir 'bad pa chen pos bzung ba ni gzhar yang sman yon gyi tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab

[\[161a.5\]]rgyal ba mchog gi chos bzung bas/_/bde dang dga' 'thob mdzod ni mang por 'gyur/_/sngon gyi rim gro bya ba 'thob 'gyur zhing /_/mi khom brgyad po ma lus zad par spong /_/'jig tshe rgyal ba mchog gi chos bzung bas/_/dper na nam mkha'i skar mas yongs

[\[161a.7\]]tu bde la longs spyod ldan/_/'jig tshe rgyal ba mchog gi chos bzung bas/_/mthu dang stobs dang ldan zhing brtson 'grus ldan/_/mi dman sa rnams kun tu rnam par rgyu/_/sangs rgyas brgya stong dag la bsnyen bkur byed/_/'jig tshe rgyal ba mchog gi chos bzung bas/_/
[\[161b.1\]]mchog tu rab mdzes gzugs ldan shes rab ldan/_/mi yi 'jig rten mchog tu bsnyen bkur 'gyur/_/rgyal po mkhas pa mdzangs pa rnams kyis bsngags/_/'jig tshe rgyal ba mchog gi chos bzung bas/_/mchog tu gzugs mdzes blta na sdug pa dang /_/skyes

[\[161b.7\]]rab kyi phyi mo glegs bam gyi phreng bar 'khod pa med na thos bsam byed pa mi 'byung la/_de med par yang sgrub pa nyams len mi 'byung bas chos yongs su 'dzin pa'i rtsa ba'ang 'di nyid kho nar shes par bya'o/_/de lta bu'i phan yon chen po dang ldan pa'i glegs bam gyi

[\[164b.7\]]bsngo ba ni/_gzhan yang dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag 'di ltar yongs su bsngo bar bya ste/_ji ltar gzugs khams gsum gyi khongs su chad pa ma yin te zhes bya ba la sogs pa gang gsungs pa yin no/_/bsod nams chen po 'byung ba'i bsngo ba'ang chung ngu dang /_'bring dang /

[\[170a.3\]]yid can 'di dag sgrol gyur cig_33_/legs byas mtha' yas mngon par spel ba'i glegs bam phyi mo rmad byung ba/_/yid bzhin nor bus phyung bur gtams pa'i sgrom mang yongs su bye 'dra 'di/_/lha yi rdzing ring gzugs su ma gyur de srid rgya 
[\[170a.4\]]mtsho'i gos can gzhir/_/skal ba can rnams chos kyi 'dod 'jo mi zad slad du rtag gyur cig_34_/gang gi drin gyis sa gsum dag na dge mtshan bya ma rtas bkod pa'i/_/bsod nams phung po gser gyi mchod sdong nyin byed bye ba'i snang ba 
[\[170a.5\]]can/_/mi dge'i mun pa rnam par snyil byed pha mtha' med par bdal ba yang /_/zad pa med par phan bde spro byed bum pa bzang po ltar gyur cig_35_/legs byas rin chen rtsol bas bsgrubs la dngos dang brgyud pas 'brel ba yi/_/skye 
[\[170a.6\]]dgu rnams kyang kun 'byung bud shing bsam yas nyid las skyes pa'i me/_/sdug bsngal rgyud du kun nas 'bar ba sred len dri yi bzhon pa can/_/rmeg med bcom nas chos kyi rgyal sar dbugs dbyung chen po thob gyur cig_36_/bdag kyang rgyal bas 
[\[170a.7\]]legs par gsungs pa'i bdud rtsis nyams stobs rdzogs gyur te/_/'gro ba rnams la rtsi sman mchog dang gter bum dpag bsam rin chen ltar/_/nyer 'tsho'i gzhi dang gtsug lag 'bum gyi shing rta chen por gyur nas kyang /_/thar mchog 
[\[170b.1\]]gnas su rgyal sras rnams dang lhan cig rab tu rol gyur cig_37_/de ltar lhag bsam chu mtsho las 'khrungs smon lam puN+Da rI ka'i tshal/_/rtag tu mi rnying mngon rlom ra ris gos pa med par gsal ba 'di/_/dus gsum gshegs pa'i 
[\[170b.2\]]'phags chen rnams kyi bzhed pa'i rjes su rab son te/_/thub pa mchog rnams dgyes pa'i zhal gyis chud mi za bar skyong gyur cig_38_/skyon rnams gtan bcom ye shes spyan mnga' drang srong che rnams bden par gsung ba'i bden pa dang /_/gang 
[\[170b.3\]]du zhi dang gang gis zhi ba 'gog lam rang bzhin 'dod chags bral ba'i bden pa dang /_/rig dang grol ba'i yon tan brgyad ldan 'phags pa'i tshogs rnams mi phyed 'dus pa'i bden pa yis/_/'di na de ring smon lam bgyis pa myur du 'grub 
[\[170b.4\]]pa'i bde legs chen po 'byung gyur cig_39_/bde bar gshegs pa'i bka' gangs can gyi brdas drangs pa'i phyi mo'i tshogs ji snyed pa par du bsgrubs pa'i tshul las nye bar brtsams pa'i gtam bzang po blo ldan mos pa'i kun+da yongs su kha bye ba'i 
[\[170b.5\]]zla 'od gzhon nu'i 'khri shing las de ltar bzhengs pa'i dgos ched phan yon bsngo smon dang bcas pa legs par bshad pa'i yal 'dab ste brgyad pa'o/_/de ltar bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab rin po che 
[\[170b.6\]]gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir 'gyur ro cog las deng sang ji tsam bzhugs pa par du bsgrubs pa'i tshul las nye bar brtsams te legs par bshad pa skabs brgyad kyi bdag nyid can 'di ni/_bsod nams mngon par 'du byed pa'i phrin las rgya chen po 'di 
[\[170b.7\]]gang gis bskrun par mdzad pa/_mi'i dbang po chos bzhin du sa skyong ba nyid kyi bka' stsal ba lhur blangs te/_'jig rten dbang phyug karma pa'i gsung las skyes pa'i slob 'bangs kyi tha shal/_gnam bskos 'jam dbyangs gong ma chen po'i 
[\[171a.1\]]lung gi kwan ting yAn thong mya'u tshi ge shir 'bod pa/_ming dngos karma bstan pa'i nyin byed gtsug lag chos kyi snang ba zhes bgyi bas/_bdag 
[\[171a.2\]]cag gi ston pa rnam 'dren shAkya'i dbang po dgongs pa zhi ba'i dbyings su mnal ba'i tshul bstan nas bgrang bya nyis stong drug brgya bcu gsum 'das pa/_chu mo glang gi lo gro bzhin 
[\[171a.3\]]zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi dus tshes bzang por/_sde bzhi dge bcu'i dpal 'byor mngon par mtho ba'i rgyal khab chen po nyid du bris pa dge legs su gyur cig/_/shu b+ha masku sarba dza ga twaM/_/
